Seaborn:

What is Seaborn and how does it differ from Matplotlib?
It is built on top of Matplotlib and provides a high-level interface for drawing attractive statistical graphics.
How do you create a categorical plot in Seaborn?
Use functions like sns.barplot(), sns.boxplot(), sns.violinplot().

How do you create pair plots?
Use sns.pairplot() for exploring relationships across the entire dataset.

26/12/2024, 2:18â€¯pm - Nisarg (Red & White): In deep learning, an optimizer is a model component that determines how well and how fast a network performs. The right optimizer can help reduce training time and improve accuracy, while the wrong one can waste time and resources. Here are some optimizers used in deep learning: 
Gradient descent
A simple and widely-used algorithm that minimizes the loss function by adjusting the model's parameters. The learning rate is a key factor in the convergence of gradient descent. 
RMSProp
Adjusts the learning rate for each weight in the model, which can help find the global minimum of the loss functions. It works well with sparse gradients and non-stationary objectives. 
Stochastic gradient descent (SGD)
A good choice when working with large datasets and simple neural network architectures. It can also be a good option when time is limited and a quick solution is needed. 
AdaGrad
Useful for handling sparse data, where some input features are missing or have low frequency. Adagrad can adaptively adjust the learning rate of each parameter. 
Mini batch gradient descent
An improvement on SGD and standard gradient descent. It updates the model parameters after every batch. 
Adadelta
An extension of Adagrad that allows for per-dimension learning rates. 
Adam optimizer
Combines the advantages of momentum and RMSprop. It calculates an adaptive learning rate for each parameter. 
SGD with momentum
Works better than the normal Stochastic Gradient Descent Algorithm.
